Audio playback lifetime audit

Goal:
  Explain NPC voice stutter/wrong speed without guessing.
  Map BSAudioManager users, locks, allocator calls, and overlap with PDD/async flush.
  This should answer whether gheap PDD freeze can retain/reuse audio objects,
  or whether audio symptoms are more likely from async flush/lock contention/VAS pressure.

======================================================================
Audio roots and known lock/wait functions
======================================================================
